49	Massachusetts Institute of Technology (MIT)	Physics	$40,331	1.44	2019-2020	4th	All students in the department receive the same salary ($3361/month) and the Student Extended  Insurance Plan, regardless of whether they are on RA, TA, internal, or external fellowship (regardless of the fellowship amount). 6399	Massachusetts Institute of Technology (MIT)	Physics	$40,331	1.44	2019-2020	4th	All students in the department receive the same salary ($3361/month) and the Student Extended  Insurance Plan, regardless of whether they are on RA, TA, internal, or external fellowship (regardless of the fellowship amount).
